</div></div></div></div><div id="section/Authentication" data-section-id="section/Authentication" class="sc-dcJsrY gzUHvb"><div class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h1 class="sc-imWYAI cILgPb"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#section/Authentication" aria-label="section/Authentication"></a>Authentication</h1></div></div><div id="section/Authentication/ApiKey" data-section-id="section/Authentication/ApiKey" class="sc-dcJsrY gzUHvb"><div class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h2 class="sc-jXbUNg fWnwAh"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#section/Authentication/ApiKey" aria-label="section/Authentication/ApiKey"></a>ApiKey</h2><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO"><p>Access to the Grist API is controlled by an Authorization header, which should contain the word &#39;Bearer&#39;, followed by a space, followed by your API key.</p>
</div><div class="sc-guJBdh ctLkki"><div class="sc-jGKxIK hHJiFY"><b>Security Scheme Type: </b><span>HTTP</span></div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO"><div class="sc-jGKxIK hHJiFY"><b>HTTP Authorization Scheme: </b><code>bearer</code></div><div class="sc-jGKxIK hHJiFY"><b>Bearer format: </b><code>Authorization: Bearer XXXXXXXXXXX</code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs" class="sc-dcJsrY gzUHvb"><div class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h1 class="sc-imWYAI cILgPb"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/orgs" aria-label="tag/orgs"></a>orgs</h1></div></div><div class="sc-fqkvVR jFELbi"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO redoc-markdown "><p>Team sites and personal spaces are called &#39;orgs&#39; in the API.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" data-section-id="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" class="sc-dcJsrY cvAPoo"><div data-section-id="operation/listOrgs" id="operation/listOrgs" class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h2 class="sc-jXbUNg fWnwAh"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs" aria-label="tag/orgs/operation/listOrgs"></a>List the orgs you have access to<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-iEXKAA jQGZcv"><button class="sc-eZYNyq knpKkQ"><span type="get" class="sc-dlWCHZ cTwxAL http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-EgOXT fVtHyw">/orgs</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR iChjUZ" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-hHOBiw jKfuBO"><div class="sc-kWtpeL fTEywo"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-ecPEgm kxVUfn"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/orgs</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-bVVIoq icSMtY"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO"><p>This enumerates all the team sites or personal areas available.</p>

class="property token string">"schema"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;{\n  \&quot;schema\&quot;: {\n    \&quot;fields\&quot;: [\n      {\n        \&quot;name\&quot;: \&quot;first_name\&quot;,\n        \&quot;type\&quot;: \&quot;string\&quot;\n        \&quot;constraints\&quot;: {\n          \&quot;required\&quot;: true\n        }\n      },\n      {\n        \&quot;name\&quot;: \&quot;age\&quot;,\n        \&quot;type\&quot;: \&quot;integer\&quot;\n      },\n    ],\n    \&quot;primaryKey\&quot;: [\n      \&quot;name\&quot;\n    ]\n  }\n}\n&quot;</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/records" data-section-id="tag/records" class="sc-dcJsrY gzUHvb"><div class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h1 class="sc-imWYAI cILgPb"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/records" aria-label="tag/records"></a>records</h1></div></div><div class="sc-fqkvVR jFELbi"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO redoc-markdown "><p>Tables contain collections of records (also called rows).</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/records/operation/listRecords" data-section-id="tag/records/operation/listRecords" class="sc-dcJsrY cvAPoo"><div data-section-id="operation/listRecords" id="operation/listRecords" class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h2 class="sc-jXbUNg fWnwAh"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/records/operation/listRecords" aria-label="tag/records/operation/listRecords"></a>Fetch records from a table<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-iEXKAA jQGZcv"><button class="sc-eZYNyq knpKkQ"><span type="get" class="sc-dlWCHZ cTwxAL http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-EgOXT fVtHyw">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR iChjUZ" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-hHOBiw jKfuBO"><div class="sc-kWtpeL fTEywo"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-ecPEgm kxVUfn"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/records</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-ibQAlb iydxeB"><div class="sc-krNlru dHDGqr"><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH sc-jaXxmE jbQuod eylnow">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-cwHptR iZRiKW" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-hwdzOV guuCvM"><span class="sc-iMTnTL gczHQi"><span class="sc-jMakVo erXvUb"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="hidden"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">hidden</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to include the hidden columns (like &quot;manualSort&quot;)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB bzckyT"><svg class="sc-cwHptR hWEnWx" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>Records from the table</p>

</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="noparse"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">noparse</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to prohibit parsing strings according to the column type.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="onmany"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">onmany</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">&quot;first&quot;</span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">&quot;none&quot;</span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">&quot;all&quot;</span> </div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Which records to update if multiple records are found to match <code>require</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>first</code> - the first matching record (default)</li>
<li><code>none</code> - do not update anything</li>
<li><code>all</code> - update all matches</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="noadd"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">noadd</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to prohibit adding records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="noupdate"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">noupdate</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to prohibit updating records.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="allow_empty_require"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">allow_empty_require</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to allow <code>require</code> in the body to be empty, which will match and update all records in the table.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-eBMEME cPThXn">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO"><p>The records to add or update. Instead of an id, a <code>require</code> object is provided, with the same structure as <code>fields</code>. If no query parameter options are set, then the operation is as follows. First, we check if a record exists matching the values specified for columns in <code>require</code>. If so, we update it by setting the values specified for columns in <code>fields</code>. If not, we create a new record with a combination of the values in <code>require</code> and <code>fields</code>, with <code>fields</code> taking priority if the same column is specified in both. The query parameters allow for variations on this behavior.</p>
</div><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv sc-Nxspf hZbWKe jXkfaY gQgOVd" kind="field" title="records"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">records</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR ivsSRP" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV">Array of </span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">objects</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB iyHUa-d" disabled=""><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGgWBj sc-gsFSXq TXHIH eDeKjd"><div><h3 class="sc-kpDqfm eBBgSB"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-bXCLTC dHowgL" string">&quot;Int&quot;</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></div></li></ul><span class="token data-section-id="tag/columns/operation/replaceColumns" class="sc-dcJsrY cvAPoo"><div data-section-id="operation/replaceColumns" id="operation/replaceColumns" class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h2 class="sc-jXbUNg fWnwAh"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/columns/operation/replaceColumns" aria-label="tag/columns/operation/replaceColumns"></a>Add or update columns of a table<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-iEXKAA jQGZcv"><button class="sc-eZYNyq knpKkQ"><span type="put" class="sc-dlWCHZ lenzxa http-verb put">put</span><span class="sc-EgOXT </div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="noupdate"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">noupdate</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to prohibit updating columns.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="replaceall"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">replaceall</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">boolean</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Set to true to remove existing columns (except the hidden ones) that are not specified in the request body.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-eBMEME cPThXn">application/json</span></h5><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO"><p>The columns to add or update. We check whether the specified column ID exists: if so, the column is updated with the provided data, otherwise a new column is created.
Also note that some query parameters alter this behavior.</p>
</div><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv sc-Nxspf hZbWKe jXkfaY gQgOVd" kind="field" title="columns"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">columns</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR ivsSRP" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV">Array of </span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">objects</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB iyHUa-d" disabled=""><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGgWBj sc-gsFSXq TXHIH eDeKjd"><div><h3 class="sc-kpDqfm eBBgSB"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-bXCLTC dHowgL" data-section-id="tag/columns/operation/deleteColumn" class="sc-dcJsrY cvAPoo"><div data-section-id="operation/deleteColumn" id="operation/deleteColumn" class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR </div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="colId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">colId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>The column id (without the starting <code>$</code>) as shown in the column configuration below the label</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB iyHUa-d" disabled=""><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>Success</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGgWBj sc-gsFSXq TXHIH eDeKjd"></div></div></div><div id="tag/data" data-section-id="tag/data" class="sc-dcJsrY gzUHvb"><div class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h1 class="sc-imWYAI cILgPb"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/data" aria-label="tag/data"></a>data</h1></div></div><div class="sc-fqkvVR jFELbi"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO redoc-markdown "><p>Work with table data, using a (now deprecated) columnar format. We now recommend the <code>records</code> endpoints.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/data/operation/getTableData" data-section-id="tag/data/operation/getTableData" class="sc-dcJsrY cvAPoo"><div data-section-id="operation/getTableData" id="operation/getTableData" class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h2 class="sc-jXbUNg fWnwAh"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/data/operation/getTableData" aria-label="tag/data/operation/getTableData"></a>Fetch data from a table<!-- --> <span type="warning" class="sc-jEACwC gWyYnj"> Deprecated </span></h2><div class="sc-iEXKAA jQGZcv"><button class="sc-eZYNyq knpKkQ"><span type="get" class="sc-dlWCHZ cTwxAL http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-EgOXT fVtHyw">/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR iChjUZ" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-hHOBiw jKfuBO"><div class="sc-kWtpeL fTEywo"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-ecPEgm kxVUfn"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/tables/{tableId}/data</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-bVVIoq icSMtY"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO"><p>Deprecated in favor of <code>records</code> endpoints. We have no immediate plans to remove these endpoints, but consider <code>records</code> a better starting point for new projects.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-ibQAlb iydxeB"><div class="sc-krNlru dHDGqr"><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH sc-jaXxmE jbQuod eylnow">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-cwHptR iZRiKW" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-hwdzOV guuCvM"><span class="sc-iMTnTL gczHQi"><span class="sc-jMakVo erXvUb"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="tableId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">tableId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>normalized table name (see <code>TABLE ID</code> in Raw Data) or numeric row ID in <code>_grist_Tables</code></p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB bzckyT"><svg class="sc-cwHptR hWEnWx" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>Cells from the table</p>

</div><div><div class="sc-fHjqPf kXaLaR"> Array </div><div class="sc-brPLxw kTlgFv"><div><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">integer</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-hmdomO fgPTUk"></div></div><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB iyHUa-d" disabled=""><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>Nothing returned</p>
</span></button></div></div></div><div class="sc-iGgWBj sc-gsFSXq TXHIH eDeKjd"><div><h3 class="sc-kpDqfm eBBgSB"> <!-- -->Request samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-bXCLTC dHowgL" data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="react-tabs__tab react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-78" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-79" tabindex="0" data-rttab="true">Payload</li></ul><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-79" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-78"><div><div class="sc-fBWQRz hEqesG"><span class="sc-bbSZdi hzinCC">Content type</span><div class="sc-fjvvzt dMqZRk">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-hCPjZK gKuDgt"><div class="sc-fXSgeo HQFTv"><div class="sc-koXPp efufqz"><button><div class="sc-jxOSlx ebiVIa">Copy</div></button></div><div class="sc-eeDRCY gTGgei sc-JrDLc hMzemk"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="array collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">101</span>,</div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">102</span>,</div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="token number">103</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">]</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments" class="sc-dcJsrY gzUHvb"><div class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h1 class="sc-imWYAI cILgPb"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/attachments" aria-label="tag/attachments"></a>attachments</h1></div></div><div class="sc-fqkvVR jFELbi"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dJWFsO redoc-markdown "><p>Documents may include attached files. Data records can refer to these using a column of type <code>Attachments</code>.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" data-section-id="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" class="sc-dcJsrY cvAPoo"><div data-section-id="operation/listAttachments" id="operation/listAttachments" class="sc-kAyceB elpaJa"><div class="sc-fqkvVR lhmVtc"><h2 class="sc-jXbUNg fWnwAh"><a class="sc-jlZhew kbdRLs" href="#tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments" aria-label="tag/attachments/operation/listAttachments"></a>List metadata of all attachments in a doc<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-iEXKAA jQGZcv"><button class="sc-eZYNyq knpKkQ"><span type="get" class="sc-dlWCHZ cTwxAL http-verb get">get</span><span class="sc-EgOXT fVtHyw">/docs/{docId}/attachments</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR iChjUZ" style="margin-right:-25px" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div aria-hidden="true" class="sc-hHOBiw jKfuBO"><div class="sc-kWtpeL fTEywo"><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"></div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-ecPEgm kxVUfn"><span>https://{subdomain}.getgrist.com/api</span>/docs/{docId}/attachments</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-ibQAlb iydxeB"><div class="sc-krNlru dHDGqr"><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH sc-jaXxmE jbQuod eylnow">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-cwHptR iZRiKW" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-hwdzOV guuCvM"><span class="sc-iMTnTL gczHQi"><span class="sc-jMakVo erXvUb"><i>ApiKey</i></span></span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="docId"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">docId</span><div class="sc-iHbSHJ sc-klVQfs jJvHFQ SbUMR">required</div></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>A string id (UUID)</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">query<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="filter"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">filter</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">filter={&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>This is a JSON object mapping column names to arrays of allowed values.  For example, to filter column <code>pet</code> for values <code>cat</code> and <code>dog</code>, the filter would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;]}</code>. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is <code>%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D</code>. See <a href="https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding">https://rosettacode.org/wiki/URL_encoding</a> for how to url-encode a string, or <a href="https://www.urlencoder.org/">https://www.urlencoder.org/</a> to try some examples. Multiple columns can be filtered. For example the filter for <code>pet</code> being either <code>cat</code> or <code>dog</code>, AND <code>size</code> being either <code>tiny</code> or <code>outrageously small</code>, would be <code>{&quot;pet&quot;: [&quot;cat&quot;, &quot;dog&quot;], &quot;size&quot;: [&quot;tiny&quot;, &quot;outrageously small&quot;]}</code>.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="sort"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">sort</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">sort=pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Order in which to return results. If a single column name is given (e.g. <code>pet</code>), results are placed in ascending order of values in that column. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special <code>manualSort</code> column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. <code>pet,age</code>). For descending order, prefix a column name with a <code>-</code> character (e.g. <code>pet,-age</code>). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. <code>pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner</code>). Available options are: <code>choiceOrder</code>, <code>naturalSort</code>, <code>emptyFirst</code>. Without the <code>sort</code> parameter, the order of results is unspecified.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="limit"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">limit</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">limit=5</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Return at most this number of rows.  A value of 0 is equivalent to having no limit.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h5 class="sc-dAlyuH jbQuod">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-dAbbOL ccPhmY"><tbody><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="X-Sort"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">X-Sort</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">string</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">pet,-age</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Same as <code>sort</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="X-Limit"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">X-Limit</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><span class="sc-cfxfcM ecSUzn"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-fxwrCY ecSUzn cdJsux">5</span></div><div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Same as <code>limit</code> query parameter.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB bzckyT"><svg class="sc-cwHptR hWEnWx" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>List of attachment metadata records. Must be a single SELECT statement, with no trailing semicolon. WITH clauses are permitted. All Grist documents are currently SQLite databases, and the SQL query is interpreted and run by SQLite, with various defensive measures. Statements that would modify the database are not supported.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv sc-Nxspf hZbWKe jXkfaY gQgOVd" kind="field" title="args"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><button aria-label="expand properties"><span class="property-name">args</span><svg class="sc-cwHptR ivsSRP" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV">Array of </span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">numbers or strings</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Parameters for the query.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td class="sc-dLMFU sc-eldPxv hZbWKe jXkfaY" kind="field" title="timeout"><span class="sc-gFqAkR eRqgPI"></span><span class="property-name">timeout</span></td><td class="sc-fPXMVe bAXEAa"><div><div><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gFAWRd ecSUzn bbMYmV"></span><span class="sc-cfxfcM sc-gmPhUn ecSUzn hUewpb">number</span></div> <div><div class="sc-eeDRCY sc-dCFHLb gTGgei dwkgVY"><p>Timeout after which operations on the document will be interrupted. Specified in milliseconds. Defaults to 1000 (1 second). This default is controlled by an optional environment variable read by the Grist app, GRIST_SQL_TIMEOUT_MSEC. The default cannot be exceeded, only reduced.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table><div><h3 class="sc-fMMURN egoxtT">Responses</h3><div><button class="sc-gdyeKB bzckyT"><svg class="sc-cwHptR hWEnWx" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg><strong class="sc-dSIIpw bpEYcE">200<!-- --> </strong><span class="sc-fhzFiK gducij"><p>The result set for the query.</p>

null.\n\n`missingValues` are strings rather than being the data type of the particular field. JSON contains characters that are not safe to place in a URL, so it is important to url-encode them.  For this example, the url-encoding is `%7B%22pet%22%3A%20%5B%22cat%22%2C%20%22dog%22%5D%7D`. For example the filter for `pet` being either `cat` or `dog`, AND `size` being either `tiny` or `outrageously small`, would be `{\"pet\": [\"cat\", \"dog\"], \"size\": [\"tiny\", \"outrageously small\"]}`.","example":"{\"pet\": [\"cat\", \"dog\"]}","required":false},"sortQueryParam":{"in":"query","name":"sort","schema":{"type":"string"},"description":"Order in which to return results. To get results in an order that was previously prepared manually in Grist, use the special `manualSort` column name. Multiple columns can be specified, separated by commas (e.g. `pet,age`). For descending order, prefix a column name with a `-` character (e.g. `pet,-age`). To include additional sorting options append them after a colon (e.g. `pet,-age:naturalSort;emptyFirst,owner`). Available options are: `choiceOrder`, `naturalSort`, `emptyFirst`. Without the `sort` parameter, the order of results is unspecified.","example":"pet,-age","required":false},"limitQueryParam":{"in":"query","name":"limit","schema":{"type":"number"},"description":"Return at most this number of rows.
